<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {

        var uniqueUpcoming = [].map.call($(".tag-btn"), function(item){
            return '&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#' + item.textContent + '" class="tag-menu-btn"&gt;' + item.textContent + '&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;';
        }).filter( function(value, index, self) {
            return self.indexOf(value) === index;
        }).join("");

        if(uniqueUpcoming !== ""){
            $(".categories&gt;li&gt;a.active + .sd-tags-list").append(uniqueUpcoming);
        }

        var PartnerTagClickHandler = function() {
            var currentItem = this.textContent;
            var isActive = $(this).hasClass('active');
            if(isActive){
                $(".tag-btn, .tag-menu-btn").removeClass("active");
                $(".tutorials-article").show();
                if(this.tagName.toUpperCase() == "BUTTON"){
                    this.blur();
                }

            }else{
                $(".tag-btn").add(".tag-menu-btn").removeClass("active").map(function(){
                    if (this.textContent == currentItem) {
                        return this;
                    }
                }).addClass("active");

                $(".tutorials-article").show().filter(function() {
                    return $(this).find(".tag-btn.active").size() === 0;
                }).hide();
            }


        };

        $(".tutorials-article").on("click", ".tag-btn", PartnerTagClickHandler);
        $(".categories").on("click", ".tag-menu-btn", PartnerTagClickHandler);
    });



</script>

                </div>
            </div>


            <div id="main-block" class="col-xs-12 col-lg-9">
                <div style="display: block;" class="content">

                    
                        <div class="article-wrapper"><h1 id="discovery-api" class="article" style="margin-right: 0px;">Discovery API</h1><p class="version-button active"><a href="/products-and-docs/apis/discovery/v2/">V 2.0</a></p><p class="version-button"><a href="/products-and-docs/apis/discovery/v1/">V 1.0</a></p></div>





<div class="article-wrapper"><div class="left-wrapper" style="margin-right: 0px;"><p class="lead article">Search and look up events, attractions, venues and classifications across all supported sources, markets and locales.</p></div><div class="aside-wrapper"><h4 id="developer-console" class="aside gray">Developer Console</h4><p>Make live API calls right now in the interactive docs:</p><p><a class="button" href="/products-and-docs/apis/interactive-console/">INTERACTIVE DOCS</a></p></div></div>







<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="overview" class="article" style="margin-right: 0px;">Overview</h2><h3 id="authentication">Authentication</h3><p>To run a successful API call, you will need to pass your API Key in the <code class="highlighter-rouge">apikey</code> query parameter. <strong>Your API Key should automatically appear in all URLs throughout this portal</strong>.</p><p>Example: <code class="highlighter-rouge">https://app.ticketmaster.com/discovery/v2/events.json?{apikey}</code></p><p>Without a valid API Key, you will receive a <code class="highlighter-rouge">401</code> Status Code with the following response:</p><div class="highlighter-rouge"><pre class="highlight"><code><span class="p">{</span><span class="w">
    </span><span class="nt">"fault"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w">
        </span><span class="nt">"faultstring"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Invalid ApiKey"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w">
        </span><span class="nt">"detail"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w">
            </span><span class="nt">"errorcode"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"oauth.v2.InvalidApiKey"</span><span class="w">
        </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
    </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
</span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
</span></code></pre>
</div><h3 id="root-url">Root URL</h3><p><code class="highlighter-rouge">https://app.ticketmaster.com/discovery/v2/</code></p><h3 id="event-sources">Event Sources</h3><p>The API provides access to content sourced from various platform, including <strong>Ticketmaster</strong>, <strong>Universe</strong>, <strong>FrontGate Tickets</strong> and <strong>Ticketmaster Resale</strong> (TMR). By default, the API returns events from all sources. To specify a specifc source(s), use the <code class="highlighter-rouge">&amp;source=</code> parameter. Multiple, comma separated values are OK.</p><h3 id="event-coverage">Event Coverage</h3><p>With over 113K+ events available in the API, coverage spans all of the following countries: <strong>United States</strong>, <strong>United Kingdom</strong>, <strong>Ireland</strong>, <strong>Australia</strong>, <strong>New Zealand</strong>, <strong>Mexico</strong> and <strong>Canada</strong>. More events and more countries are added on continious basis.</p><p><img alt="event map" src="/assets/img/products-and-docs/map.png" /></p><h3 id="examples">Examples</h3><p><strong>Get a list of all events in the United States</strong>
<code class="highlighter-rouge">https://app.ticketmaster.com/discovery/v2/events.json?countryCode=US&amp;{apikey}</code></p><p><strong>Search for events sourced by Universe in the United States with keyword “devjam”</strong>
<code class="highlighter-rouge">https://app.ticketmaster.com/discovery/v2/events.json?keyword=devjam&amp;source=universe&amp;countryCode=US&amp;{apikey}</code></p><p><strong>Search for music events in the Los Angeles area</strong>
<code class="highlighter-rouge">https://app.ticketmaster.com/discovery/v2/events.json?classificationName=music&amp;dmaId=324&amp;{apikey}</code></p><p><strong>Get a list of all events for Adele in Canada</strong>
<code class="highlighter-rouge">https://app.ticketmaster.com/discovery/v2/events.json?attractionId=K8vZ917Gku7&amp;countryCode=CA&amp;{apikey}</code></p></div>



































<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="srch-events-v2" class="article console-link underline">Search Events<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Returns the 20 most recent events for the authenticating user.</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/events.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">version</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The API Version.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">format</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">API Response Format.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“json”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="query-parameters">Query parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>

      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>

      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">keyword</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">A string to search against event’s name. Partial word will not be found. ex: <code class="highlighter-rouge">keyword=Mado</code> will not found event with name: Madonna</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>

      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>

    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">radius</code></td>

      <td style="text-align: left">“25”</td>

      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>

      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>

      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>

<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="event-details-v2" class="article console-link underline">Get Event Details<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Returns the event detail by event ID.</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/events/{id}.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-1">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">version</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The API Version.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">id</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Event ID. Required.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“1A4ZAZyGkeUYKaO”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">format</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">API Response Format.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“json”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="query-parameters-1">Query parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">locale</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The event locale, including country and localization. Values: “”, “en-us”, “en-gb”, “en-ca”, “es-us”, “en-mx”, “es-mx”, “en-au”, “en-nz”, “fr-fr”, “fr-ca”.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“en-us”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="response-structure-1">Response structure:</h3><div class="nested-list-wrapper jstree jstree-2 jstree-default" role="tree"><ul class="jstree-container-ul jstree-children"><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j2_1" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_embedded</code> (object) - container for related items.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j2_60" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_links</code> (object) - links to event.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j2_69" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">classifications</code> (array) - classifications.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j2_81" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">dates</code> (object) - dates of event.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" id="j2_101" class="jstree-node  jstree-leaf"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">id</code> (string) - id of event.</span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j2_102" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">images</code> (array) - images.

<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="event-img-v2" class="article console-link underline">Get Event Images<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Returns all the images for an event by ID. If an event does not have an image for a supported resolution, the event’s major category image will be returned instead.</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/events/{id}/images.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-2">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">version</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The API Version.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">id</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Event ID. Required.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“1A4ZAZyGkeUYKaO”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">format</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">API Response Format.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“json”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="query-parameters-2">Query parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">locale</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The event locale, including country and localization. Values: “”, “en-us”, “en-gb”, “en-ca”, “es-us”, “en-mx”, “es-mx”, “en-au”, “en-nz”, “fr-fr”, “fr-ca”.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“en-us”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="response-structure-2">Response structure:</h3><div class="nested-list-wrapper jstree jstree-3 jstree-default" role="tree"><ul class="jstree-container-ul jstree-children"><li role="treeitem" id="j3_1" class="jstree-node  jstree-leaf"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">type</code> (string) - type of images set</span></li><li role="treeitem" id="j3_2" class="jstree-node  jstree-leaf"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">id</code> (string) - id of event</span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j3_3" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">images</code> (array) - images.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j3_10" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed jstree-last"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_links</code> (object) - links to images data set.

    </span><span class="nt">"self"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w">  </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w">
      </span><span class="nt">"href"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"/discovery/v2/events/k7vGFKzleBdwS/images?locale=en-us"</span><span class="w">
    </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
  </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
</span><span class="p">}</span></code></pre></figure></div></div>





<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="search-attractions-v2" class="article console-link underline">Search Attractions<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Search Attractions!</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/attractions.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-3">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">version</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The API Version.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">format</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">API Response Format.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“json”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="query-parameters-3">Query parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">keyword</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">A string to search against events, attractions and venues. The keyword will be checked against titles, descriptions, names and other logical fields that describe any of these data objects.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">locale</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The event locale, including country and localization. Values: “”, “en-us”, “en-gb”, “en-ca”, “es-us”, “en-mx”, “es-mx”, “en-au”, “en-nz”, “fr-fr”, “fr-ca”.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">size</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The number of events returned in the API response.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“20”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">page</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The page for paginating through the results.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“1”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">sort</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The search sort criteria. Values: “name,desc”, “name,asc”.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="response-structure-3">Response structure:</h3><div class="nested-list-wrapper jstree jstree-4 jstree-default" role="tree"><ul class="jstree-container-ul jstree-children"><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j4_1" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_embedded</code> (object) - container attractions.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j4_32" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_links</code> (object) - links to attractions data set.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j4_40" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed jstree-last"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">page</code> (object) - information about current page in data source.

<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="attraction-details-v2" class="article console-link underline">Get Attraction Details<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Search Attractions!</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/attractions/{id}.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-4">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>

      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>

      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">id</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Attraction ID.</td>

      <td style="text-align: left">“K8vZ917G7x0”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>

        </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"KnvZfZ7vAeA"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w">
        </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Rock"</span><span class="w">
      </span><span class="p">},</span><span class="w">
      </span><span class="nt">"subGenre"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w">  </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w">
        </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"KZazBEonSMnZfZ7v6F1"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w">
        </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Pop"</span><span class="w">
      </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
    </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
  </span><span class="p">],</span><span class="w">
  </span><span class="nt">"_links"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w">  </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w">
    </span><span class="nt">"self"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w">  </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w">
      </span><span class="nt">"href"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"/discovery/v2/attractions/K8vZ9175BhV?locale=en-us"</span><span class="w">
    </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
  </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w">
</span><span class="p">}</span></code></pre></figure></div></div>





<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="search-classifications-v2" class="article console-link underline">Search Classifications<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Search Classifications!</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/classifications.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-5">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">version</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The API Version.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">format</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">API Response Format.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“json”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="query-parameters-5">Query parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">keyword</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">A string to search against events, attractions and venues. The keyword will be checked against titles, descriptions, names and other logical fields that describe any of these data objects.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">classificationID </code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">classification ID</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">size</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The number of events returned in the API response.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“20”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">page</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The page for paginating through the results.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“1”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">sort</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The search sort criteria. Values: “”, “name,desc”, “name,asc”.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="response-structure-5">Response structure:</h3><div class="nested-list-wrapper jstree jstree-6 jstree-default" role="tree"><ul class="jstree-container-ul jstree-children"><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j6_1" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_embedded</code> (object) - container for classifications.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j6_27" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_links</code> (object) - links to classifications data sets.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j6_34" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed jstree-last"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">page</code> (object) - information about current page in data source.

<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="classifications-details-v2" class="article console-link underline">Get Classification Details<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Returns the classification detail by ID.</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/classifications/{id}.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-6">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">version</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The API Version.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">id</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Category ID.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“KZFzniwnSyZfZ7v7na”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">format</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">API Response Format.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“json”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="query-parameters-6">Query parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Description</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Type</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">locale</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The event locale, including country and localization. Values: “”, “en-us”, “en-gb”, “en-ca”, “es-us”, “en-mx”, “es-mx”, “en-au”, “en-nz”, “fr-fr”, “fr-ca”.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left"> </td>
      <td style="text-align: left">No</td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table></div><h3 id="response-structure-6">Response structure:</h3><div class="nested-list-wrapper jstree jstree-7 jstree-default" role="tree"><ul class="jstree-container-ul jstree-children"><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j7_1" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">_links</code> (object) - links to classifications data sets.
    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j7_4" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed jstree-last"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">segment</code> (object) - segment.
    </span></li></ul></div></div><div class="aside-wrapper tab-panel-offset"><a class="active-lang" href="javascript:void(0)">JavaScript</a><blockquote class="aside lang-selector" tabindex="-1">
  <p><a href="#js" class="active">JavaScript</a>
<a href="#curl">cURL</a></p>
</blockquote><figure class="highlight tab-content tab-0 tab-active"><div class="copy-btn" rel="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-original-title="Copy to Clipboard" data-clipboard-text="$.ajax({
  type:&quot;GET&quot;,

<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="search-venues-v2" class="article console-link underline">Search Venues<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Search Venues!</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/venues.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-7">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>

    </span></li><li role="treeitem" aria-expanded="false" id="j8_39" class="jstree-node  jstree-closed jstree-last"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-ocl"></i><span class="jstree-anchor" href="#"><i class="jstree-icon jstree-themeicon"></i><code class="highlighter-rouge">page</code> (object) - information about current page in data source.
    </span></li></ul></div></div><div class="aside-wrapper tab-panel-offset"><a class="active-lang" href="javascript:void(0)">JavaScript</a><blockquote class="aside lang-selector" tabindex="-1">

<div class="article-wrapper"><h2 id="venue-details-v2" class="article console-link underline">Get Venue Details<a class="console-btn" href="#"></a></h2><div class="left-wrapper"><p><strong>Method:</strong> GET.
Authentication required.
Returns the venue detail by ID.</p><p class="code red">discovery/{version}/venues/{id}.{format}</p><h3 id="url-parameters-8">URL parameters:</h3><div class="table-wrapper"><table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th style="text-align: left">Parameter</th>

      <th style="text-align: left">Default Value</th>
      <th style="text-align: left">Required</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">version</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">The API Version.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“v2”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">id</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Venue ID.</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">string</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">“KovZpZAFnIEA”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td style="text-align: left"><code class="highlighter-rouge">format</code></td>
      <td style="text-align: left">API Response Format.</td>

      <td style="text-align: left">“json”</td>
      <td style="text-align: left">Yes</td>
    </tr>

<script>
    var userKey = sessionStorage.getItem('tk-api-key');

    function replaceText(selector, text, newText, flags) {
        var matcher = new RegExp(text, flags);
        $(selector).each(function () {
            var $this = $(this);
            if (!$this.children().length)
                $this.text($this.text().replace(matcher, newText));
        });
    }

    if(userKey !== null) {
        replaceText('*', '\{apikey\}', "apikey=" + sessionStorage.getItem('tk-api-key'), 'g');
    }

    $(window).on('login',function(){
        replaceText('*', '\{apikey\}', "apikey=" + sessionStorage.getItem('tk-api-key'), 'g');
    });
</script>
